# AWS4 Shape Catalog for draw.io

A complete catalog of 930 unique AWS4 shapes extracted from the
`mxgraph.aws4` stencil library. Every style string is copy-paste ready
for draw.io XML generation.

## Shape naming convention

All AWS shapes live under the `mxgraph.aws4.*` namespace. Two patterns
exist:

**Resource icons** use `shape=mxgraph.aws4.resourceIcon` with a
separate `resIcon=mxgraph.aws4.<SERVICE>` attribute. These render the
icon inside a category-coloured rounded square.

**Product icons** set `shape=mxgraph.aws4.<SERVICE>` directly with no
`resIcon`. These render the bare service glyph.

To derive a shape not listed here, convert the service name to
`lower_snake_case` and substitute it into the appropriate template.
Check the draw.io aws4 stencil source if unsure of the exact
identifier.

---

## Colour conventions

| Category | Hex | Services |
| ---------------- | --------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| Compute | `#ED7100` | EC2, Lambda, ECS, EKS, Fargate, etc. |
| Storage | `#7AA116` | S3, EBS, EFS, Glacier, etc. |
| Database | `#C925D1` | RDS, Aurora, DynamoDB, ElastiCache, etc. |
| Networking | `#8C4FFF` | VPC, CloudFront, Route 53, API GW, etc. |
| Security | `#DD344C` | IAM, Cognito, WAF, Shield, KMS, etc. |
| App Integration | `#E7157B` | SQS, SNS, EventBridge, Step Functions |
| Management | `#E7157B` | CloudWatch, CloudTrail, Config, etc. |
| Analytics | `#8C4FFF` | Kinesis, Athena, Glue, EMR, etc. |
| Developer Tools | `#C925D1` | CodePipeline, CodeBuild, etc. |
| AI/ML | `#01A88D` | SageMaker, Bedrock, etc. |

---

## Group / container styles

These are used for the dashed or solid boundary boxes that wrap sets of
resources. All groups use `container=1;collapsible=0;pointerEvents=0;`.

### AWS Cloud

- **Style:** `points=[[0,0],[0.25,0],[0.5,0],[0.75,0],[1,0],[1,0.25],[1,0.5],[1,0.75],[1,1],[0.75,1],[0.5,1],[0.25,1],[0,1],[0,0.75],[0,0.5],[0,0.25]];outlineConnect=0;gradientColor=none;html=1;whiteSpace=wrap;fontSize=12;fontStyle=0;shape=mxgraph.aws4.group;grIcon=mxgraph.aws4.group_aws_cloud;strokeColor=#232F3E;fillColor=none;verticalAlign=top;align=left;spacingLeft=30;fontColor=#232F3E;dashed=0;container=1;pointerEvents=0;collapsible=0;`

---

## Edge style

Preferred style from AWS reference diagrams:

```text
edgeStyle=orthogonalEdgeStyle;rounded=0;orthogonalLoop=1;
jettySize=auto;html=1;endArrow=open;endFill=0;strokeWidth=2;
```

- Use `rounded=0;` for AWS edge routing.
- Stroke colour: `#545B64` (AWS dark grey) or `#808080` (neutral).
- For fan-out patterns, use `edgeStyle=elbowEdgeStyle;`.
- See `references/templates/aws/` examples for style guidance.
